msg:The location is very good, close to the subway entrance, and only 5 stops away from Suzhou Railway Station. There are many choices of shopping malls and restaurants within 1 kilometer of the surrounding area, and it can be reached by walking and public transportation. The hotel just opened in July this year. The facilities are very new and there is no peculiar smell. The mattress is of average quality, too soft and has poor support. The shower head is a bit small. Although other facilities are new, the materials and workmanship are average. I stayed here when it was new. It's still okay to stay, there are free drinks and welcome fruits, and free upgrades for less than 500 yuan, which is very cost-effective. After renewing the lease for 2 days, the price slightly increased to less than 600 yuan. The hotel is connected to the Pan Pacific and shares two swimming pools and gardens. The indoor swimming pool was not open for maintenance when I stayed, and there were swimming classes from outside. The pool was small and crowded with people, and there were many accompanying parents, and the seats were full. Man, this is not good. Logically speaking, a swimming pool like this should not be open to the public. It is really impossible to control the time period and length of the time limit. Nowadays, it really affects the interests of hotel guests. It is worth mentioning that the Panmen attraction is right behind the hotel. You can enter it directly from the garden with your room card for free, which is just like the back garden of the hotel. There are some indoor antique-themed photo spots in the hotel that are quite interesting. The hotel breakfast is average, with a fairly complete range but not many varieties, and the taste is average. The attitude of the service staff is very good, but many interns are not very proficient in their work.
